# All modules

MCP Kotlin SDK
==============

Kotlin SDK for the Model Context Protocol (MCP). This is a Kotlin Multiplatform library that helps you build MCP clients and servers that speak the same protocol and share the same types. The SDK focuses on clarity, small building blocks, and first‑class coroutine support.

Use the umbrella `kotlin-sdk` artifact when you want a single dependency that brings the core types plus both client and server toolkits. If you only need one side, depend on `kotlin-sdk-client` or `kotlin-sdk-server` directly.

Gradle (Kotlin DSL):

    dependencies {    // Convenience bundle with everything you need to start    implementation("io.modelcontextprotocol:kotlin-sdk:<version>")    // Or pick modules explicitly    implementation("io.modelcontextprotocol:kotlin-sdk-client:<version>")    implementation("io.modelcontextprotocol:kotlin-sdk-server:<version>")}

Content copied to clipboard

Module kotlin-sdk-core
----------------------

Foundational, platform‑agnostic pieces:

*   Protocol data model and JSON serialization (kotlinx.serialization)
    
*   Request/response and notification types used by both sides of MCP
    
*   Coroutine‑friendly protocol engine and utilities
    
*   Transport abstractions shared by client and server
    

You typically do not use `core` directly in application code; it is pulled in by the client/server modules. Use it explicitly if you only need the protocol types or plan to implement a custom transport.

Module kotlin-sdk-client
------------------------

High‑level client API for connecting to an MCP server and invoking its tools, prompts, and resources. Ships with several transports:

*   WebSocketClientTransport – low latency, full‑duplex
    
*   SSEClientTransport – Server‑Sent Events over HTTP
    
*   StdioClientTransport – CLI‑friendly stdio bridge
    
*   StreamableHttpClientTransport – simple HTTP streaming
    

A minimal client:

    val client = Client(    clientInfo = Implementation(name = "sample-client", version = "1.0.0"))client.connect(WebSocketClientTransport("ws://localhost:8080/mcp"))val tools = client.listTools()val result = client.callTool(    name = "echo",    arguments = mapOf("text" to "Hello, MCP!"))

Content copied to clipboard

Module kotlin-sdk-server
------------------------

Lightweight server toolkit for hosting MCP tools, prompts, and resources. It provides a small, composable API and ready‑to‑use transports:

*   StdioServerTransport – integrates well with CLIs and editors
    
*   SSE/WebSocket helpers for Ktor – easy HTTP deployment
    

Register tools and run over stdio:

    val server = Server(    serverInfo = Implementation(name = "sample-server", version = "1.0.0"),    options = ServerOptions(ServerCapabilities()))server.addTool(    name = "echo",    description = "Echoes the provided text") { request ->    // Build and return a CallToolResult from request.arguments    // (see CallToolResult and related types in kotlin-sdk-core)    /* ... */}// Bridge the protocol over stdioval transport = StdioServerTransport(    inputStream = kotlinx.io.files.Path("/dev/stdin").source(),    outputStream = kotlinx.io.files.Path("/dev/stdout").sink())// Start transport and wire it with the server using provided helpers in the SDK.

Content copied to clipboard

For HTTP deployments, use the Ktor extensions included in the module to expose an MCP WebSocket or SSE endpoint with a few lines of code.

# kotlin-sdk-client

kotlin-sdk-client
=================

The Model Context Protocol (MCP) Kotlin SDK client module provides a multiplatform implementation for connecting to and interacting with MCP servers.

Features
--------

*   Cross-platform support for JVM, WASM, JS, and Native
    
*   Built-in support for multiple transport protocols (stdio, SSE, WebSocket)
    
*   Type-safe API for resource management and server interactions
    

Packages
--------

[io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/index.html)

Link copied to clipboard

common

---

# kotlin-sdk-server

kotlin-sdk-server
=================

The server module provides core server-side functionality for the Model Context Protocol (MCP) Kotlin SDK. This module includes essential parts for writing MCP server applications.

Features
--------

*   Server-side request handling
    
*   Model context management
    
*   Protocol implementation
    
*   Integration utilities
    

For detailed usage instructions and examples, please refer to the [documentation](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/blob/main/README.md)
.

Packages
--------

[io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/index.html)

Link copied to clipboard

common

commonjsjvmnativewasmJs

The MCP Kotlin SDK Core module provides fundamental functionality for interacting with Model Context Protocol (MCP). This module serves as the foundation for building MCP-enabled applications in Kotlin.

Client transport for Streamable HTTP: this implements the MCP Streamable HTTP transport specification. It will connect to a server using HTTP POST for sending messages and HTTP GET with Server-Sent Events for receiving messages.

# ClientCapabilities

ClientCapabilities
==================

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [ClientCapabilities](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-capabilities/index.html)
(val sampling: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null, val roots: [ClientCapabilities.Roots](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-capabilities/-roots/index.html)
? = null, val elicitation: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null, val experimental: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null)([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/capabilities.kt#L50)
)

Capabilities that a client may support.

Known capabilities are defined here, but this is not a closed set: any client can define its own additional capabilities through the [experimental](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-capabilities/--root--.html)
 field.

The presence of a capability object (non-null value) indicates that the client supports that capability.

Members

Constructors
------------

? = null, elicitation: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null, experimental: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null)

SSEClientTransport

# GetPromptResult

GetPromptResult
===============

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [GetPromptResult](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-get-prompt-result/index.html)
(val messages: [List](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.collections/-list/index.html)
<[PromptMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-prompt-message/index.html)
\>, val description: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
? = null, val meta: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null) : [ServerResult](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-server-result/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/prompts.kt#L181)
)

The server's response to a [GetPromptRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-get-prompt-request/index.html)
 from the client.

Contains the prompt's messages and optional description. If the prompt was a template, the messages will have arguments already substituted.

Members

Constructors
------------

[messages](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-get-prompt-result/messages.html)

Link copied to clipboard

val [messages](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-get-prompt-result/messages.html)
: [List](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.collections/-list/index.html)
<[PromptMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-prompt-message/index.html)
\>

The list of messages that make up this prompt. Each message has a role (e.g., "user", "assistant") and content.

Prompt
======

A prompt or prompt template that the server offers.

Prompts can be static messages or templates that accept arguments for dynamic content generation.

# GetPromptRequest

GetPromptRequest
================

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [GetPromptRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-get-prompt-request/index.html)
(val params: [GetPromptRequestParams](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-get-prompt-request-params/index.html)
) : [ClientRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-request/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/prompts.kt#L112)
)

Used by the client to get a prompt provided by the server.

Prompts can be static text or templates that accept arguments. When arguments are provided, the server will substitute them into the prompt template before returning the result.

MembersMembers & Extensions

# StdioClientTransport

StdioClientTransport
====================

class [StdioClientTransport](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/index.html)
 @[JvmOverloads](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.jvm/-jvm-overloads/index.html) constructor(input: Source, output: Sink, error: Source? = null, sendChannel: [Channel](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.coroutines/kotlinx-coroutines-core/kotlinx.coroutines.channels/-channel/index.html)
<[JSONRPCMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-message/index.html)
\> = Channel(Channel.BUFFERED), classifyStderr: ([String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
) -> [StdioClientTransport.StderrSeverity](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/-stderr-severity/index.html)
 = { DEBUG }) : [AbstractTransport](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-abstract-transport/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-client/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/client/StdioClientTransport.kt#L85)
)

A transport implementation for JSON-RPC communication over standard I/O streams.

Reads JSON-RPC messages from [input](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/--root--.html)
 and writes messages to [output](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/--root--.html)
. Optionally monitors [error](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/--root--.html)
 stream for stderr output with configurable severity handling.

Usage Example
-------------

    val process = ProcessBuilder("mcp-server").start()val transport = StdioClientTransport(    input = process.inputStream.asSource().buffered(),    output = process.outputStream.asSink().buffered(),    error = process.errorStream.asSource().buffered()) { stderrLine ->    when {        stderrLine.contains("error", ignoreCase = true) -> StderrSeverity.FATAL        stderrLine.contains("warning", ignoreCase = true) -> StderrSeverity.WARNING        else -> StderrSeverity.INFO    }}transport.start()

Content copied to clipboard

#### Parameters

input

The input stream where messages are received.

output

The output stream where messages are sent.

error

Optional error stream for stderr monitoring.

sendChannel

Channel for outbound messages. Default: buffered channel (implementation-default capacity).

classifyStderr

Callback to classify stderr lines. Return [StderrSeverity.FATAL](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/-stderr-severity/-f-a-t-a-l/index.html)
 to fail transport, or StderrSeverity.WARNING / StderrSeverity.INFO / StderrSeverity.DEBUG to log, or StderrSeverity.IGNORE to discard. Default value: StderrSeverity.DEBUG.

#### See also

[MCP Specification](https://modelcontextprotocol.io/specification/2025-06-18/basic/transports#stdio)

[Channel.Factory.BUFFERED](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.coroutines/kotlinx-coroutines-core/kotlinx.coroutines.channels/-channel/-factory/-b-u-f-f-e-r-e-d.html)

Members

Constructors
------------

Link copied to clipboard

<[JSONRPCMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-message/index.html)
\> = Channel(Channel.BUFFERED), classifyStderr: ([String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
) -> [StdioClientTransport.StderrSeverity](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/-stderr-severity/index.html)
 = { DEBUG })

# CallToolRequest

CallToolRequest
===============

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [CallToolRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-call-tool-request/index.html)
(val params: [CallToolRequestParams](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-call-tool-request-params/index.html)
) : [ClientRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-request/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/tools.kt#L140)
)

Used by the client to invoke a tool provided by the server.

Tools allow servers to expose functionality that clients (and LLMs) can call. Examples include file operations, API calls, database queries, or any other server-side operations.

# JSONRPCMessage

JSONRPCMessage
==============

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)
(with = [JSONRPCMessagePolymorphicSerializer::class](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-message-polymorphic-serializer/index.html)
)

sealed interface [JSONRPCMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-message/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/jsonRpc.kt#L84)
)

Base interface for all JSON-RPC 2.0 messages.

All messages in the MCP protocol follow the JSON-RPC 2.0 specification.

#### Inheritors

[JSONRPCEmptyMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-empty-message/index.html)

# Protocol

Protocol
========

abstract class [Protocol](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-protocol/index.html)
(options: [ProtocolOptions](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-protocol-options/index.html)
?)([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/shared/Protocol.kt#L161)
)

Implements MCP protocol framing on top of a pluggable transport, including features like request/response linking, notifications, and progress.

Optional annotations for the client. The client can use annotations to inform how objects are used or displayed.

The client can use annotations to inform how objects are used or displayed.

val [lastModified](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-annotations/last-modified.html)
: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
?

The moment the resource was last modified, as an ISO 8601 formatted string (e.g., "2025-01-12T15:00:58Z"). Examples: last activity timestamp in an open file, timestamp when the resource was attached, etc.

[priority](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-annotations/priority.html)

Link copied to clipboard

val [priority](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-annotations/priority.html)
: [Double](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-double/index.html)
?

Describes how important this data is for operating the server. A value of 1.0 means "most important" and indicates that the data is effectively required, while 0.0 means "least important" and indicates that the data is entirely optional. Should be a value between 0.0 and 1.0.

# Implementation

Implementation
==============

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [Implementation](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-implementation/index.html)
(val name: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
, val version: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
, val title: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
? = null, val websiteUrl: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)

<[Icon](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/index.html)
\>? = null)([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/capabilities.kt#L26)
)

Describes an MCP (Model Context Protocol) implementation.

This metadata helps clients identify and display information about servers or clients, including their name, version, and optional branding elements like icons and website links.

# Client

Client
======

open class [Client](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-client/index.html)
(clientInfo: [Implementation](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-implementation/index.html)
, options: [ClientOptions](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-client-options/index.html)
 = ClientOptions()) : [Protocol](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-protocol/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-client/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/client/Client.kt#L110)
)

An MCP client on top of a pluggable transport.

The client automatically performs the initialization handshake with the server when [connect](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-client/connect.html)
 is called. After initialization, [serverCapabilities](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-client/server-capabilities.html)
 and [serverVersion](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-client/server-version.html)
 provide details about the connected server.

You can extend this class with custom request/notification/result types if needed.

#### Parameters

clientInfo

Information about the client implementation (name, version).

options

Configuration options for this client.

------------

# StderrSeverity

StderrSeverity
==============

enum [StderrSeverity](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/-stderr-severity/index.html)
 : [Enum](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-enum/index.html)
<[StdioClientTransport.StderrSeverity](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/-stderr-severity/index.html)
\> ([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-client/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/client/StdioClientTransport.kt#L112)
)

Severity classification for stderr messages.

*   [FATAL](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/-stderr-severity/-f-a-t-a-l/index.html)
    : Calls error handler and terminates transport.
    
*   [WARNING](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/-stderr-severity/-w-a-r-n-i-n-g/index.html)
    : Logs at WARN level, transport continues.
    
*   [INFO](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/-stderr-severity/-i-n-f-o/index.html)
    : Logs at INFO level, transport continues.
    
*   [DEBUG](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/-stderr-severity/-d-e-b-u-g/index.html)
    : Logs at DEBUG level, transport continues.
    
*   [IGNORE](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/-stderr-severity/-i-g-n-o-r-e/index.html)
    : Discards message silently, transport continues.

A known resource that the server is capable of reading.

Resources represent data sources such as files, database entries, API responses, or other structured data that can be read by clients.

# StreamableHttpClientTransport

StreamableHttpClientTransport
=============================

class [StreamableHttpClientTransport](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-streamable-http-client-transport/index.html)
(client: [HttpClient](https://api.ktor.io/ktor-client/ktor-client-core/io.ktor.client/-http-client/index.html)
, url: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)

 = {}) : [AbstractTransport](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-abstract-transport/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-client/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/client/StreamableHttpClientTransport.kt#L61)
)

Client transport for Streamable HTTP: this implements the MCP Streamable HTTP transport specification. It will connect to a server using HTTP POST for sending messages and HTTP GET with Server-Sent Events for receiving messages.

# ReadResourceRequest

ReadResourceRequest
===================

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [ReadResourceRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-read-resource-request/index.html)
(val params: [ReadResourceRequestParams](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-read-resource-request-params/index.html)
) : [ClientRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-request/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/resources.kt#L249)
)

Sent from the client to the server to read a specific resource URI.

The server will return the resource's contents, which can be either text or binary data.

MembersMembers & Extensions

# ReadResourceResult

ReadResourceResult
==================

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [ReadResourceResult](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-read-resource-result/index.html)
(val contents: [List](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.collections/-list/index.html)
<[ResourceContents](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-resource-contents/index.html)
\>, val meta: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null) : [ServerResult](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-server-result/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/resources.kt#L304)
)

The server's response to a [ReadResourceRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-read-resource-request/index.html)
 from the client.

Contains the resource contents, which can be a mix of text and binary data. A single resource can return multiple content blocks if it contains multiple parts.

<[ResourceContents](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-resource-contents/index.html)
\>

The contents of the resource. Can include text content (with MIME type and text data) or binary/blob content (with MIME type and Base64-encoded data). Multiple content blocks can be returned for resources with multiple parts.

# Tool

Tool
====

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [Tool](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool/index.html)
(val name: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
, val inputSchema: [ToolSchema](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool-schema/index.html)
, val description: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
? = null, val outputSchema: [ToolSchema](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool-schema/index.html)
? = null, val title: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
? = null, val annotations: [ToolAnnotations](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool-annotations/index.html)
? = null, val icons: [List](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.collections/-list/index.html)
<[Icon](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/index.html)
\>? = null, val meta: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null) : [WithMeta](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-with-meta/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/tools.kt#L61)
)

Definition for a tool the client can call.

Tools allow servers to expose functionality that can be invoked by clients and LLMs. Each tool has a name, description, and schema defining its input (and optionally output) parameters.

**Display name precedence order:** [title](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool/--root--.html)
 → [annotations](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool/--root--.html)
.[title](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool/--root--.html)
 → [name](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool/--root--.html)

Optional additional tool information providing hints about tool behavior. All properties in [ToolAnnotations](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool-annotations/index.html)
 are hints and not guaranteed to provide a faithful description of tool behavior.

: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
?

A human-readable description of the tool and when to use it. Clients can use this to improve the LLM's understanding of available tools. It can be thought of like a "hint" to the model.

[icons](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool/icons.html)

\>?

Optional set of sized icons that clients can display in their user interface. Clients MUST support at least PNG and JPEG formats. Clients SHOULD also support SVG and WebP formats.

The programmatic identifier for this tool. Intended for logical use and API identification. Used as a display name fallback if both [title](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool/--root--.html)

[outputSchema](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool/output-schema.html)

val [outputSchema](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool/output-schema.html)
: [ToolSchema](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool-schema/index.html)

An optional JSON Schema object defining the structure of the tool's output returned in the [structuredContent](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-call-tool-result/structured-content.html)
 field of a [CallToolResult](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-call-tool-result/index.html)
. Must be an object type schema if provided.

?

Optional human-readable display name for this tool. Intended for UI and end-user contexts, optimized to be easily understood even by those unfamiliar with domain-specific terminology. Note: For Tool specifically, [annotations](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool/--root--.html)
.[title](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-tool/--root--.html)
 takes precedence over this field.

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

# mcpClient

mcpClient
=========

@[ExperimentalMcpApi](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk/-experimental-mcp-api/index.html)

suspend fun [mcpClient](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/mcp-client.html)
(clientInfo: [Implementation](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-implementation/index.html)
, clientOptions: [ClientOptions](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-client-options/index.html)
 = ClientOptions(), transport: [Transport](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-transport/index.html)
): [Client](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-client/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-client/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/client/Client.kt#L86)
)

Initializes and connects an MCP client using the provided clientInfo [Implementation](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-implementation/index.html)
, client options, and transport mechanism.

#### Return

An instance of [Client](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-client/index.html)
 that is connected and ready for use with the specified transport.

#### Parameters

clientInfo

The implementation details of the MCP client, including its name, version, and other metadata.

clientOptions

Optional client configuration settings, such as supported capabilities and strict enforcement options. Defaults to a new instance of ClientOptions.

transport

The transport mechanism used for communication.

---

# ExperimentalMcpApi

ExperimentalMcpApi
==================

@[Target](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.annotation/-target/index.html)
(allowedTargets = \[[AnnotationTarget.CLASS](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.annotation/-annotation-target/-c-l-a-s-s/index.html)\
, [AnnotationTarget.ANNOTATION\_CLASS](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.annotation/-annotation-target/-a-n-n-o-t-a-t-i-o-n_-c-l-a-s-s/index.html)\
, [AnnotationTarget.PROPERTY](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.annotation/-annotation-target/-p-r-o-p-e-r-t-y/index.html)\
, [AnnotationTarget.FIELD](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.annotation/-annotation-target/-f-i-e-l-d/index.html)\
, [AnnotationTarget.LOCAL\_VARIABLE](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.annotation/-annotation-target/-l-o-c-a-l_-v-a-r-i-a-b-l-e/index.html)\
, [AnnotationTarget.VALUE\_PARAMETER](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.annotation/-annotation-target/-v-a-l-u-e_-p-a-r-a-m-e-t-e-r/index.html)\
, [AnnotationTarget.CONSTRUCTOR](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.annotation/-annotation-target/-c-o-n-s-t-r-u-c-t-o-r/index.html)\
, [AnnotationTarget.FUNCTION](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.annotation/-annotation-target/-f-u-n-c-t-i-o-n/index.html)\
, [AnnotationTarget.PROPERTY\_GETTER](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.annotation/-annotation-target/-p-r-o-p-e-r-t-y_-g-e-t-t-e-r/index.html)\
, [AnnotationTarget.PROPERTY\_SETTER](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.annotation/-annotation-target/-p-r-o-p-e-r-t-y_-s-e-t-t-e-r/index.html)\
, [AnnotationTarget.TYPEALIAS](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.annotation/-annotation-target/-t-y-p-e-a-l-i-a-s/index.html)\
\])

annotation class [ExperimentalMcpApi](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk/-experimental-mcp-api/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/ExperimentalMcpApi.kt#L57)
)

Annotation marking an API as experimental and subject to changes or removal in the future.

This annotation is used to signal that a particular element, such as a class, function, or property, is part of an experimental API. Such APIs may not be stable, and their usage requires opting in explicitly.

Users of the annotated API must explicitly accept the opt-in requirement to ensure they are aware of the potential instability or unfinished nature of the API.

Targets that can be annotated include:

*   Classes
    
*   Annotation classes
    
*   Properties
    
*   Fields
    
*   Local variables
    
*   Value parameters
    
*   Constructors
    
*   Functions
    
*   Property getters
    
*   Property setters
    
*   Type aliases

---

# CallToolResult

CallToolResult
==============

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [CallToolResult](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-call-tool-result/index.html)
(val content: [List](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.collections/-list/index.html)
<[ContentBlock](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-content-block/index.html)
\>, val isError: [Boolean](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-boolean/index.html)
? = null, val structuredContent: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null, val meta: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null) : [ServerResult](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-server-result/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/tools.kt#L203)
)

The server's response to a [CallToolRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-call-tool-request/index.html)
.

Contains the result of the tool execution, which can be successful or an error.

**Important error handling:**

*   Errors that originate from the **tool itself** SHOULD be reported inside the result object with [isError](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-call-tool-result/--root--.html)
     set to true, NOT as an MCP protocol-level error response. This allows the LLM to see that an error occurred and potentially self-correct.
    
*   Errors in **finding the tool**, unsupported operations, or other exceptional conditions SHOULD be reported as MCP protocol-level error responses.
    

Members

Constructors

[isError](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-call-tool-result/is-error.html)

: [Boolean](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-boolean/index.html)
?

Whether the tool call ended in an error. If not set, this is assumed to be false (the call was successful). When true, the [content](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-call-tool-result/--root--.html)
 should describe the error that occurred.

[structuredContent](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-call-tool-result/structured-content.html)

# ServerCapabilities

ServerCapabilities
==================

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [ServerCapabilities](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-server-capabilities/index.html)
(val tools: [ServerCapabilities.Tools](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-server-capabilities/-tools/index.html)
? = null, val resources: [ServerCapabilities.Resources](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-server-capabilities/-resources/index.html)
? = null, val prompts: [ServerCapabilities.Prompts](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-server-capabilities/-prompts/index.html)
? = null, val logging: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null, val completions: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null, val experimental: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null)([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/capabilities.kt#L94)
)

Capabilities that a server may support.

Known capabilities are defined here, but this is not a closed set: any server can define its own additional capabilities through the [experimental](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-server-capabilities/--root--.html)
 field.

The presence of a capability object (non-null value) indicates that the server supports that capability.

# Server

Server
======

open class [Server](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-server/index.html)
(serverInfo: [Implementation](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-implementation/index.html)
, options: [ServerOptions](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-server-options/index.html)
, instructionsProvider: () -> [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
? = null, block: [Server](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-server/index.html)
.() -> [Unit](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-unit/index.html)
 = {})([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-server/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/server/Server.kt#L78)
)

An MCP server is responsible for storing features and handling new connections.

This server automatically responds to the initialization flow as initiated by the client. You can register tools, prompts, and resources using [addTool](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-server/add-tool.html)
, [addPrompt](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-server/add-prompt.html)
, and [addResource](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-server/add-resource.html)
. The server will then automatically handle listing and retrieval requests from the client.

In case the server supports feature list notification or resource substitution, the server will automatically send notifications for all connected clients. Currently, after subscription to a resource, the server will NOT send the subscription confirmation as this response schema is not defined in the protocol.

#### Parameters

serverInfo

Information about this server implementation (name, version).

options

Configuration options for the server.

instructionsProvider

Optional provider for instructions from the server to the client about how to use this server. The provider is called each time a new session is started to support dynamic instructions.

block

A block to configure the mcp server.

Members

Constructors

# SseServerTransport

SseServerTransport
==================

class [SseServerTransport](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-sse-server-transport/index.html)
(endpoint: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
, session: [ServerSSESession](https://api.ktor.io/ktor-client/ktor-server-sse/io.ktor.server.sse/-server-s-s-e-session/index.html)
) : [AbstractTransport](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-abstract-transport/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-server/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/server/SSEServerTransport.kt#L34)
)

Server transport for SSE: this will send messages over an SSE connection and receive messages from HTTP POST requests.

Creates a new SSE server transport, which will direct the client to POST messages to the relative or absolute URL identified by `_endpoint`.

Content copied to clipboard

The client's response to a sampling/create\_message request from the server. The client should inform the user before returning the sampled message to allow them to inspect the response (human in the loop) and decide whether to allow the server to see it.

# StreamableHttpServerTransport

StreamableHttpServerTransport
=============================

class [StreamableHttpServerTransport](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-streamable-http-server-transport/index.html)
(enableJsonResponse: [Boolean](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-boolean/index.html)
 = false, enableDnsRebindingProtection: [Boolean](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-boolean/index.html)
 = false, allowedHosts: [List](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.collections/-list/index.html)
<[String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
\>? = null, allowedOrigins: [List](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.collections/-list/index.html)
<[String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
\>? = null, eventStore: [EventStore](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-event-store/index.html)
? = null, retryIntervalMillis: [Long](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-long/index.html)
? = null) : [AbstractTransport](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-abstract-transport/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-server/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/server/StreamableHttpServerTransport.kt#L83)
)

Server transport for Streamable HTTP: this implements the MCP Streamable HTTP transport specification. It supports both SSE streaming and direct HTTP responses.

In stateful mode:

*   Session ID is generated and included in response headers
    
*   Session ID is always included in initialization responses
    
*   Requests with invalid session IDs are rejected with 404 Not Found
    
*   Non-initialization requests without a session ID are rejected with 400 Bad Request
    
*   State is maintained in-memory (connections, message history)
    

In stateless mode:

*   No Session ID is included in any responses
    
*   No session validation is performed
    

#### Parameters

enableJsonResponse

If true, the server will return JSON responses instead of starting an SSE stream. This can be useful for simple request/response scenarios without streaming. Default is false (SSE streams are preferred).

enableDnsRebindingProtection

Enable DNS rebinding protection (requires allowedHosts and/or allowedOrigins to be configured). Default is false for backwards compatibility.

allowedHosts

List of allowed host header values for DNS rebinding protection. If not specified, host validation is disabled.

allowedOrigins

List of allowed origin header values for DNS rebinding protection. If not specified, origin validation is disabled.

eventStore

Event store for resumability support If provided, resumability will be enabled, allowing clients to reconnect and resume messages

retryIntervalMillis

Retry interval (in milliseconds) advertised via SSE priming events to hint the client when to reconnect. Applies only when an [eventStore](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-streamable-http-server-transport/--root--.html)
 is configured. Defaults to `null` (no retry hint).

fun [setOnSessionClosed](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-streamable-http-server-transport/set-on-session-closed.html)
(block: ([String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
) -> [Unit](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-unit/index.html)
?)

A callback for session close events This is called when the server closes a session due to a DELETE request. Useful in cases when you need to clean up resources associated with the session. Note that this is different from the transport closing, if you are handling HTTP requests from multiple nodes you might want to close each StreamableHTTPServerTransport after a request is completed while still keeping the session open/running.

[setOnSessionInitialized](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-streamable-http-server-transport/set-on-session-initialized.html)

(block: ([String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
) -> [Unit](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-unit/index.html)
?)

A callback for session initialization events This is called when the server initializes a new session. Useful in cases when you need to register multiple mcp sessions and need to keep track of them.

Function that generates a session ID for the transport. The session ID SHOULD be globally unique and cryptographically secure (e.g., a securely generated UUID, a JWT, or a cryptographic hash)

The client's response to a [CreateMessageRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-create-message-request/index.html)
 from the server.

The client should inform the user before returning the sampled message, to allow them to inspect the response (human in the loop) and decide whether to allow the server to see it.

The name of the model that generated the message (e.g., "claude-3-opus-20240229", "gpt-4-turbo-preview"). This helps the server understand which model was used.

[role](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-create-message-result/role.html)

: [Role](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-role/index.html)

The role of the message sender. Typically [Role.Assistant](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-role/-assistant/index.html)
 for LLM-generated responses.

The reason why sampling stopped, if known. Common values: "end\_turn", "max\_tokens", "stop\_sequence", "content\_filter"

# JSONRPCNotification

JSONRPCNotification
===================

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [JSONRPCNotification](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-notification/index.html)
(val method: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
, val params: [JsonElement](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-element/index.html)
? = null) : [JSONRPCMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-message/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/jsonRpc.kt#L165)
)

A notification which does not expect a response.

Notifications are fire-and-forget messages. They do not have an `id` and the recipient does not send any response (neither success nor error).

Examples: progress updates, resource change notifications, log messages.

Members

Constructors
------------

[JSONRPCNotification](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-notification/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-notification.html)

Link copied to clipboard

constructor(method: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
, params: [JsonElement](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-element/index.html)
? = null)

# Roots

Roots
=====

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [Roots](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-capabilities/-roots/index.html)
(val listChanged: [Boolean](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-boolean/index.html)
? = null)([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/capabilities.kt#L73)
)

Indicates that the client supports listing roots.

Roots are the top-level directories or locations that the server can access. When present (non-null), the server can query available roots and optionally receive notifications when the roots list changes.

Members

Constructors
------------

[Roots](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-capabilities/-roots/-roots.html)

Link copied to clipboard

constructor(listChanged: [Boolean](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-boolean/index.html)
? = null)

Properties
----------

[listChanged](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-capabilities/-roots/list-changed.html)

Link copied to clipboard

val [listChanged](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-capabilities/-roots/list-changed.html)
: [Boolean](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-boolean/index.html)
?

Whether the client supports notifications for changes to the roots list. If true, the client will send notifications when roots are added or removed.

# JSONRPCRequest

JSONRPCRequest
==============

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [JSONRPCRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-request/index.html)
 @[JvmOverloads](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.jvm/-jvm-overloads/index.html) constructor(val id: [RequestId](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-request-id/index.html)
 = RequestId(Uuid.random().toHexString()), val method: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
, val params: [JsonElement](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-element/index.html)
? = null) : [JSONRPCMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-message/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/jsonRpc.kt#L112)
)

A request that expects a response.

Requests are identified by a unique [id](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-request/--root--.html)
 and specify a [method](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-request/--root--.html)
 to invoke. The server or client (depending on a direction) must respond with either a [JSONRPCResponse](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-response/index.html)
 or [JSONRPCError](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-error/index.html)
 that has the same [id](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-request/--root--.html)
.

MembersMembers & Extensions

Link copied to clipboard

, params: [JsonElement](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-element/index.html)

? = null)

Constructs a JSON-RPC request using a numerical ID, method name, and optional parameters.

# RequestResult

RequestResult
=============

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)
(with = [RequestResultPolymorphicSerializer::class](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-request-result-polymorphic-serializer/index.html)

sealed interface [RequestResult](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-request-result/index.html)
 : [WithMeta](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-with-meta/index.html)

# getStreamIdForEventId

getStreamIdForEventId
=====================

abstract suspend fun [getStreamIdForEventId](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-event-store/get-stream-id-for-event-id.html)
(eventId: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
): [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
?([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-server/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/server/EventStore.kt#L32)
)

Returns the stream ID associated with [eventId](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-event-store/get-stream-id-for-event-id.html)
, or null if the event is unknown. Default implementation is a no-op which disables extra validation during replay.

# InitializeRequest

InitializeRequest
=================

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [InitializeRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-initialize-request/index.html)
(val params: [InitializeRequestParams](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-initialize-request-params/index.html)
) : [ClientRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-request/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/initialize.kt#L20)
)

This request is sent from the client to the server when it first connects, asking it to begin initialization.

The initialize request is the first message exchanged in the MCP protocol handshake. It allows the client to communicate its capabilities and protocol version to the server, and receive the server's capabilities in response.

# replayEventsAfter

replayEventsAfter
=================

abstract suspend fun [replayEventsAfter](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-server/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.server/-event-store/replay-events-after.html)
(lastEventId: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
, sender: suspend (eventId: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
, message: [JSONRPCMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-message/index.html)
) -> [Unit](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-unit/index.html)
): [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-server/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/server/EventStore.kt#L23)
)

Replays events after the specified event ID

#### Return

The stream ID for the replayed events

#### Parameters

lastEventId

The last event ID that was received

sender

Function to send events

# enforceStrictCapabilities

enforceStrictCapabilities
=========================

var [enforceStrictCapabilities](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-protocol-options/enforce-strict-capabilities.html)
: [Boolean](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-boolean/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/shared/Protocol.kt#L85)
)

Whether to restrict emitted requests to only those that the remote side has indicated that they can handle, through their advertised capabilities.

Note that this DOES NOT affect checking of _local_ side capabilities, as it is considered a logic error to mis-specify those.

Currently, this defaults to false, for backwards compatibility with SDK versions that did not advertise capabilities correctly. In the future, this will default to true.

---

)

A progress token, used to associate progress notifications with the original request.

# InitializeResult

InitializeResult
================

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [InitializeResult](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-initialize-result/index.html)
(val protocolVersion: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
 = LATEST\_PROTOCOL\_VERSION, val capabilities: [ServerCapabilities](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-server-capabilities/index.html)
, val serverInfo: [Implementation](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-implementation/index.html)
, val instructions: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
? = null, val meta: [JsonObject](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-json/kotlinx.serialization.json/-json-object/index.html)
? = null) : [ServerResult](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-server-result/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/initialize.kt#L91)
)

After receiving an [InitializeRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-initialize-request/index.html)
 from the client, the server sends this response.

The server communicates its chosen protocol version, capabilities, and optional instructions for how to effectively use its features.

[instructions](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-initialize-result/instructions.html)

Link copied to clipboard

val [instructions](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-initialize-result/instructions.html)
: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
?

Optional instructions describing how to use the server and its features. Clients can use this to improve the LLM's understanding of available tools, resources, etc. It can be thought of as a "hint" to the model. For example, this information MAY be added to the system prompt to help the LLM make better use of the server's capabilities.

# JSONRPCError

JSONRPCError
============

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [JSONRPCError](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-error/index.html)
(val id: [RequestId](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-request-id/index.html)
?, val error: [RPCError](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-r-p-c-error/index.html)
) : [JSONRPCMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-message/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/jsonRpc.kt#L205)
)

A response to a request that indicates an error occurred.

Sent in response to a [JSONRPCRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-request/index.html)
 when the method execution fails. The [id](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-error/--root--.html)
 must match the [id](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-error/--root--.html)
 of the original request.

# RequestId

RequestId
=========

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)
(with = [RequestIdPolymorphicSerializer::class](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-request-id-polymorphic-serializer/index.html)

sealed interface [RequestId](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-request-id/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/jsonRpc.kt#L27)
)

A uniquely identifying ID for a request in JSON-RPC.

# JSONRPCResponse

JSONRPCResponse
===============

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [JSONRPCResponse](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-response/index.html)
(val id: [RequestId](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-request-id/index.html)
, val result: [RequestResult](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-request-result/index.html)
 = EmptyResult()) : [JSONRPCMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-message/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/jsonRpc.kt#L185)
)

A successful (non-error) response to a request.

Sent in response to a [JSONRPCRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-request/index.html)
 when the method execution succeeds. The [id](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-response/--root--.html)
 must match the [id](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-response/--root--.html)
 of the original request.

# PromptArgument

PromptArgument
==============

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [PromptArgument](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-prompt-argument/index.html)
(val name: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)

Describes an argument that a prompt can accept.

Arguments allow prompts to be templated with user-provided values.

 is not provided, this should be used as a fallback display name.

# Icon

Icon
====

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [Icon](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/index.html)
(val src: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
, val mimeType: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
? = null, val sizes: [List](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.collections/-list/index.html)
<[String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
\>? = null, val theme: [Icon.Theme](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/-theme/index.html)
? = null)([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/common.kt#L86)
)

An optionally sized icon that can be displayed in a user interface.

Icons help clients provide visual branding and identification for MCP implementations.

**Security considerations:**

*   Consumers SHOULD ensure URLs serving icons are from the same domain as the client/server or a trusted domain to prevent malicious content.
    
*   Consumers SHOULD take appropriate precautions when rendering SVGs as they can contain executable JavaScript. Consider sanitizing SVG content or rendering in isolated contexts.
    

Members

Constructors
------------

, mimeType: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
? = null, sizes: [List](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.collections/-list/index.html)
<[String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
\>? = null, theme: [Icon.Theme](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/-theme/index.html)
? = null)

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

enum [Theme](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/-theme/index.html)
 : [Enum](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-enum/index.html)
<[Icon.Theme](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/-theme/index.html)
\>

The theme context for which an icon is designed.

Properties
----------

[mimeType](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/mime-type.html)

Link copied to clipboard

val [mimeType](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/mime-type.html)
: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
?

Optional MIME type override if the source MIME type is missing or generic. For example, "image/png", "image/jpeg", or "image/svg+xml". Useful when the URL doesn't include a file extension or uses a generic MIME type.

[sizes](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/sizes.html)

Link copied to clipboard

val [sizes](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/sizes.html)
: [List](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.collections/-list/index.html)
<[String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
\>?

Optional array of strings that specify sizes at which the icon can be used. Each string should be in WxH format (e.g., "48x48", "96x96") or "any" for scalable formats like SVG. If not provided, the client should assume that the icon can be used at any size.

[src](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/src.html)

Link copied to clipboard

val [src](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/src.html)
: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)

A standard URI pointing to an icon resource. Maybe an HTTP/HTTPS URL or a data: URI with Base64-encoded image data. Example: "https://example.com/icon.png" or "data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KG..."

[theme](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/theme.html)

Link copied to clipboard

val [theme](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/theme.html)
: [Icon.Theme](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/-theme/index.html)
?

Optional specifier for the theme this icon is designed for. [Theme.Light](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/-theme/-light/index.html)
 indicates the icon is designed for a light background, [Theme.Dark](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-icon/-theme/-dark/index.html)
 indicates the icon is designed for a dark background. If not provided, the client should assume the icon can be used with any theme.

# ListPromptsRequest

ListPromptsRequest
==================

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [ListPromptsRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-list-prompts-request/index.html)
(val params: [PaginatedRequestParams](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-paginated-request-params/index.html)
? = null) : [ClientRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-request/index.html)
, [PaginatedRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-paginated-request/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/prompts.kt#L201)
)

Sent from the client to request a list of prompts and prompt templates the server has.

This request supports pagination through the cursor parameter. If the server has many prompts, it may return a subset along with a cursor to fetch the next page.
