# connect

connect
=======

open suspend fun [connect](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-protocol/connect.html)
(transport: [Transport](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-transport/index.html)
)([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/shared/Protocol.kt#L237)
)

Attaches to the given transport, starts it, and starts listening for messages.

The Protocol object assumes ownership of the Transport, replacing any callbacks that have already been set, and expects that it is the only user of the Transport instance going forward.

---

# PromptMessage

PromptMessage
=============

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [PromptMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-prompt-message/index.html)
(val role: [Role](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-role/index.html)
, val content: [ContentBlock](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-content-block/index.html)
)([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/prompts.kt#L76)
)

Describes a message returned as part of a prompt.

This is similar to SamplingMessage, but also supports the embedding of resources from the MCP server.

Members

Constructors
------------

The server's response to a [ListPromptsRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-list-prompts-request/index.html)
 from the client.

Returns the available prompts and prompt templates, along with pagination information if there are more results available.

# onError

onError
=======

open override fun [onError](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-abstract-transport/on-error.html)
(block: ([Throwable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-throwable/index.html)
) -> [Unit](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-unit/index.html)
)([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/shared/AbstractTransport.kt#L33)
)

Callback for when an error occurs.

Note that errors are not necessarily fatal; they are used for reporting any kind of exceptional condition out of a band.

[onResumptionToken](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-transport-send-options/on-resumption-token.html)

Link copied to clipboard

val [onResumptionToken](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-transport-send-options/on-resumption-token.html)
: ([String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
) -> [Unit](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-unit/index.html)

a callback that is invoked when the resumption token changes, if supported by the transport. This allows clients to persist the latest token for potential reconnection.

[relatedRequestId](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-transport-send-options/related-request-id.html)

Link copied to clipboard

: [RequestId](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-request-id/index.html)
?

if present, `relatedRequestId` is used to indicate to the transport which incoming request to associate this outgoing message with.

[resumptionToken](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-transport-send-options/resumption-token.html)

Link copied to clipboard

val [resumptionToken](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-transport-send-options/resumption-token.html)
: [String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
?

the resumption token used to continue long-running requests that were interrupted. This allows clients to reconnect and continue from where they left off, if supported by the transport.

# ListResourcesRequest

ListResourcesRequest
====================

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [ListResourcesRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-list-resources-request/index.html)
(val params: [PaginatedRequestParams](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-paginated-request-params/index.html)
? = null) : [ClientRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-request/index.html)
, [PaginatedRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-paginated-request/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/resources.kt#L189)
)

Sent from the client to request a list of resources the server has.

Resources are data sources that the server can provide access to, such as files, database entries, API responses, or other structured data.

MembersMembers & Extensions

# StdioClientTransport

StdioClientTransport
====================

@[JvmOverloads](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin.jvm/-jvm-overloads/index.html)

constructor(input: Source, output: Sink, error: Source? = null, sendChannel: [Channel](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.coroutines/kotlinx-coroutines-core/kotlinx.coroutines.channels/-channel/index.html)
<[JSONRPCMessage](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-j-s-o-n-r-p-c-message/index.html)
\> = Channel(Channel.BUFFERED), classifyStderr: ([String](https://kotlinlang.org/api/core/kotlin-stdlib/kotlin/-string/index.html)
) -> [StdioClientTransport.StderrSeverity](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/-stderr-severity/index.html)
 = { DEBUG })([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-client/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/client/StdioClientTransport.kt#L85)
)

#### Parameters

input

The input stream where messages are received.

output

The output stream where messages are sent.

error

Optional error stream for stderr monitoring.

sendChannel

Channel for outbound messages. Default: buffered channel (implementation-default capacity).

classifyStderr

Callback to classify stderr lines. Return [StderrSeverity.FATAL](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-client/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.client/-stdio-client-transport/-stderr-severity/-f-a-t-a-l/index.html)
 to fail transport, or StderrSeverity.WARNING / StderrSeverity.INFO / StderrSeverity.DEBUG to log, or StderrSeverity.IGNORE to discard. Default value: StderrSeverity.DEBUG.

---

# request

=======

suspend fun <[T](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-protocol/request.html)
 : [RequestResult](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-request-result/index.html)
\> [request](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-protocol/request.html)
(request: [Request](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-request/index.html)
, options: [RequestOptions](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-request-options/index.html)
? = null): [T](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.shared/-protocol/request.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/shared/Protocol.kt#L439)
)

Sends a request and waits for a response.

Do not use this method to emit notifications! Use notification() instead.

# ListResourceTemplatesRequest

ListResourceTemplatesRequest
============================

@[Serializable](https://kotlinlang.org/api/kotlinx.serialization/kotlinx-serialization-core/kotlinx.serialization/-serializable/index.html)

data class [ListResourceTemplatesRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-list-resource-templates-request/index.html)
(val params: [PaginatedRequestParams](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-paginated-request-params/index.html)
? = null) : [ClientRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-client-request/index.html)
, [PaginatedRequest](https://modelcontextprotocol.github.io/kotlin-sdk/kotlin-sdk-core/io.modelcontextprotocol.kotlin.sdk.types/-paginated-request/index.html)
([source](https://github.com/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin-sdk/tree/main/kotlin-sdk-core/src/commonMain/kotlin/io/modelcontextprotocol/kotlin/sdk/types/resources.kt#L431)
)

Sent from the client to request a list of resource templates the server has.

Resource templates are parameterized resource URIs that can be instantiated with specific argument values. For example, a template like `file:///{path}` allows clients to construct URIs for any file path.

404
===

**File not found**

The site configured at this address does not contain the requested file.

If this is your site, make sure that the filename case matches the URL as well as any file permissions.  
For root URLs (like `http://example.com/`) you must provide an `index.html` file.

 for more information about using **GitHub Pages**.
